	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of stage names</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Wikimedia list article</div>
<p>This <b>list of stage names</b> lists names used by those in the entertainment industry, alphabetically by their <a href="/wiki/Stage_name" title="Stage name">stage name</a>'s surname, followed by their birth name. Individuals who dropped their last name and substituted their middle name as their last name are listed. In many cases, performers have legally changed their name to their stage name.<sup id="cite_ref-Pseudonyms_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pseudonyms-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><b>Note:</b> Many cultures have their own naming customs and systems (Chinese, Japanese, Korean, Arabic, Hungarian, Indian and others), some rather intricate. Minor changes or alterations, including reversing Eastern-style formats, do not in and of themselves qualify as stage names, and should not normally be included. For example, <a href="/wiki/Bj%C3%B6rk" title="Björk">Björk</a>, whose stage name appears to be an original creation, is part of her full Icelandic name, Björk Guðmundsdóttir. Her second name is a <a href="/wiki/Patronymic" title="Patronymic">patronymic</a> instead of a family name, following <a href="/wiki/Icelandic_name" title="Icelandic name">Icelandic naming conventions</a>. "Björk" is not a stage name but how any Icelander would refer to her, casually or formally.
</p><p>People are <b>not</b> listed here if they fall into one or more of the following categories:
</p>
<ul><li>Those who have more than one family name, provided at least one is represented in the professional name. This is especially common with people from Spanish and/or Portuguese-speaking countries and the Philippines.
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Baddeley" title="Hermione Baddeley">Hermione Baddeley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jacqueline_Bisset" title="Jacqueline Bisset">Jacqueline Bisset</a>, <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Guest" title="Christopher Guest">Christopher Guest</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Sangster" class="mw-redirect" title="Thomas Sangster">Thomas Sangster</a>, <a href="/wiki/Richard_Todd" title="Richard Todd">Richard Todd</a>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dd>For more information, see <a href="/wiki/Spanish_naming_customs" title="Spanish naming customs">Spanish naming customs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_American_naming_customs" class="mw-redirect" title="Hispanic American naming customs">Hispanic American naming customs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Filipino_name" title="Filipino name">Filipino names</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_name" title="Portuguese name">Portuguese names</a>.</dd></dl>
<ul><li>Those who changed their surname due primarily to marriage:
<ul><li><b>Living:</b> <i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria Beckham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sheena_Easton" title="Sheena Easton">Sheena Easton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cheryl_Ladd" title="Cheryl Ladd">Cheryl Ladd</a>, <a href="/wiki/Susan_Sarandon" title="Susan Sarandon">Susan Sarandon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jada_Pinkett_Smith" title="Jada Pinkett Smith">Jada Pinkett Smith</a>.</li>
<li><b>Dead:</b> <i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Cheryl_Barrymore" title="Cheryl Barrymore">Cheryl Barrymore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Phyllis_Diller" title="Phyllis Diller">Phyllis Diller</a>, <a href="/wiki/Edith_Head" title="Edith Head">Edith Head</a>, <a href="/wiki/Linda_McCartney" title="Linda McCartney">Linda McCartney</a>, <a href="/wiki/Estelle_Reiner" title="Estelle Reiner">Estelle Reiner</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who changed their surname due to <a href="/wiki/Adoption" title="Adoption">adoption</a> or legal name change <i>prior to</i> entering the entertainment industry:
<ul><li><b>Living:</b> <i>Examples</i> Dame <a href="/wiki/Julie_Andrews" title="Julie Andrews">Julie Andrews</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Elle_Macpherson" title="Elle Macpherson">Elle Macpherson</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Frances_McDormand" title="Frances McDormand">Frances McDormand</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Louis_Tomlinson" title="Louis Tomlinson">Louis Tomlinson</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Steven_Van_Zandt" title="Steven Van Zandt">Steven Van Zandt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Dead:</b> <i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Nancy_Reagan" title="Nancy Reagan">Nancy Davis</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Joan_Fontaine" title="Joan Fontaine">Joan Fontaine</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Charlton_Heston" title="Charlton Heston">Charlton Heston</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Madeline_Kahn" title="Madeline Kahn">Madeline Kahn</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Alan_Thicke" title="Alan Thicke">Alan Thicke</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>Those known by generational nicknames:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Trey_Anastasio" title="Trey Anastasio">Trey Anastasio</a> (whose full name is Ernest Joseph Anastasio III), <a href="/wiki/Noah_Beery_Jr." title="Noah Beery Jr.">Noah Beery Jr.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Noah_Beery_Sr." title="Noah Beery Sr.">Noah Beery Sr.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lon_Chaney_Jr." title="Lon Chaney Jr.">Lon Chaney Jr.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pops_Staples" title="Pops Staples">Pops Staples</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those referred or known publicly and/or professionally by an amended forename (substantial changes, indirect nicknames, etc.):
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Tori_Amos" title="Tori Amos">Tori Amos</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Carradine" title="David Carradine">David Carradine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hattie_Jacques" title="Hattie Jacques">Hattie Jacques</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Sellers" title="Peter Sellers">Peter Sellers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Billy_Wilder" title="Billy Wilder">Billy Wilder</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who may be popularly, though not professionally, known by a nickname, such as <a href="/wiki/Robert_John_%22Mutt%22_Lange" title="Robert John &quot;Mutt&quot; Lange">Robert John "Mutt" Lange</a>.</li>
<li>Those whose stage forename is a middle name:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Sean_Connery" title="Sean Connery">Sean Connery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ashton_Kutcher" title="Ashton Kutcher">Ashton Kutcher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paul_McCartney" title="Paul McCartney">Paul McCartney</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marie_Osmond" title="Marie Osmond">Marie Osmond</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Willis" title="Bruce Willis">Bruce Willis</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Nault&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Eden Nault (page does not exist)">Eden Nault</a> – these are their real middle names, not stage names.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who changed only a middle or second name, or who switched their first and middle names:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Halle_Berry" title="Halle Berry">Halle Berry</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Clayton-Thomas" title="David Clayton-Thomas">David Clayton-Thomas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_J._Fox" title="Michael J. Fox">Michael J. Fox</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Michael_Glaser" title="Paul Michael Glaser">Paul Michael Glaser</a>, <a href="/wiki/Phil_Spector" title="Phil Spector">Phil Spector</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who adopted a pseudo-<a href="/wiki/Nobiliary_particle" title="Nobiliary particle">nobiliary particle</a>, prefix, suffix, hyphenation or other diacritic/symbol:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/John_D%27Aquino" title="John D&#39;Aquino">John D'Aquino</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dawn_O%27Porter" title="Dawn O&#39;Porter">Dawn O'Porter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lars_von_Trier" title="Lars von Trier">Lars von Trier</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who simplified their name(s) by the removal of a genuine particle(s), prefix, suffix, hyphenation or other diacritic/symbol:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Dirk_Bogarde" title="Dirk Bogarde">Dirk Bogarde</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tabby_Callaghan" title="Tabby Callaghan">Tabby Callaghan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lyn_Christie" title="Lyn Christie">Lyn Christie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frank_Tashlin" title="Frank Tashlin">Frank Tashlin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Ustinov" title="Peter Ustinov">Peter Ustinov</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who changed the spelling of a surname to either ensure proper pronunciation or due to name conflicts in Actors Equity (or other acting unions), resulting in a name which is basically the same phonetically as the original surname:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Don_Ameche" title="Don Ameche">Don Ameche</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Blunt" title="James Blunt">James Blunt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marvin_Gaye" title="Marvin Gaye">Marvin Gaye</a>, <a href="/wiki/Julie_Newmar" title="Julie Newmar">Julie Newmar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gloria_Stuart" title="Gloria Stuart">Gloria Stuart</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those who changed their name(s) due to change in sexual gender or identity, or due to dysphoria or other recognized gender-related issue, or drag performers:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Courtney_Act" title="Courtney Act">Courtney Act</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alexis_Arquette" title="Alexis Arquette">Alexis Arquette</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lili_Elbe" title="Lili Elbe">Lili Elbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dame_Edna_Everage" title="Dame Edna Everage">Dame Edna Everage</a>, <a href="/wiki/Holly_Woodlawn" title="Holly Woodlawn">Holly Woodlawn</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Those whose stage name consists of a single word, not including those commonly referred to by their surname:
<ul><li>See <i><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_one-word_stage_names" title="List of one-word stage names">List of one-word stage names</a></b></i></li></ul></li>
<li>Those who changed their names for religious reasons:
<ul><li>See <i><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_converts_to_Islam" title="List of converts to Islam">List of converts to Islam</a></b></i></li></ul></li>
<li>Those who adopted a <a href="/wiki/Matriname" title="Matriname">matriname</a>:
<ul><li>See <i><b><a href="/wiki/List_of_people_who_adopted_matrilineal_surnames" title="List of people who adopted matrilineal surnames">List of people who adopted matrilineal surnames</a></b></i></li></ul></li>
<li>Those who changed their name(s) due to other or unknown reasons:
<ul><li><i>Examples</i> <a href="/wiki/Vondie_Curtis-Hall" title="Vondie Curtis-Hall">Vondie Curtis-Hall</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Betty_Huntley-Wright" title="Betty Huntley-Wright">Betty Huntley-Wright</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Scout_Taylor-Compton" title="Scout Taylor-Compton">Scout Taylor-Compton</a>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<p>The following <b>are</b> listed here for the following reasons:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Tupac_Shakur" title="Tupac Shakur">Tupac Shakur</a> <b>is</b> listed here, but under the stage name 2Pac. He was born either Lesane Parish Crooks or Parish Lesane Crooks, depending on the source, but his name was changed in early childhood to Tupac Amaru Shakur.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Elton_John" title="Elton John">Elton John</a> <b>is</b> listed here because he used the name professionally before he legally adopted it in 1972.</li></ul>
<p><br />
</p>

<h2><span id="0.E2.80.939_and_other_stage_names_which_do_not_begin_with_English_alphabetic_characters"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="0–9_and_other_stage_names_which_do_not_begin_with_English_alphabetic_characters">0–9 and other stage names which do not begin with English alphabetic characters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_stage_names&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: 0–9 and other stage names which do not begin with English alphabetic characters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Tupac_Shakur" title="Tupac Shakur">2Pac</a> – Tupac Amaru Shakur (born as either Parish Lesane Crooks or Lesane Parish Crooks)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/50_Cent" title="50 Cent">50 Cent</a> – Curtis James Jackson III</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/6ix9ine" title="6ix9ine">6ix9ine</a> – Daniel Hernandez</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carlos_Cadona" title="Carlos Cadona">6025</a> – Carlos Cadona</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/75_Cents" class="mw-redirect" title="75 Cents">75 Cents</a> – Ladislav Demeterffy</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2_Chainz" title="2 Chainz">2 Chainz</a> – Tauheed Epps</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%CE%9C-Ziq" class="mw-redirect" title="Μ-Ziq">μ-Ziq</a> – Michael Paradinas</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="A">A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_stage_names&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>Aa–Aq</b>
</p>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Dominique_A" title="Dominique A">Dominique A</a> – Dominique Ané</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Angela_Aames" title="Angela Aames">Angela Aames</a> – Lois Marie Tlustos</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Willie_Aames" title="Willie Aames">Willie Aames</a> – Albert William Upton</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Caroline_Aaron" title="Caroline Aaron">Caroline Aaron</a> – Caroline Sidney Abady</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lee_Aaron" title="Lee Aaron">Lee Aaron</a> – Karen Lynn Greening</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russ_Abbot" title="Russ Abbot">Russ Abbot</a> – Russell Roberts</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abdullah_the_Butcher" title="Abdullah the Butcher">Abdullah the Butcher</a> (a.k.a. "The Madman from The Sudan") – Lawrence Robert Shreve</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Abi_Ann" class="mw-redirect" title="Abi Ann">Abi Ann</a> – Abigail Dawn Ann Hoffman</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Victoria_Abril" title="Victoria Abril">Victoria Abril</a> – Victoria Mérida Rojas</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ace_Frehley" title="Ace Frehley">Ace Frehley</a> – Paul Frehley</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goodman_Ace" title="Goodman Ace">Goodman Ace</a> – Goodman Aiskowitz</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Johnny_Ace" title="Johnny Ace">Johnny Ace (singer)</a> – John Marshall Alexander, Jr.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_Laurinaitis" title="John Laurinaitis">Johnny Ace (wrestler)</a> – John Hodger Laurinaitis</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="L">L</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_stage_names&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: L">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="O">O</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_stage_names&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: O">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">

</li>
<li id="cite_note-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-2">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Julie Andrews was born Julia Elizabeth Wells, but took the name Andrews when she moved in with her stepfather as a child.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Elle Macpherson was born Eleanor Nancy Gow, but was assigned her stepfather's surname (see <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://business.timesonline.co.uk/tol/business/industry_sectors/consumer_goods/article3601582.ece">"Elle Macpherson looks good with Intimates"</a>)</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Frances McDormand was born Cindy Ann Smith but was adopted at one and a half years of age by Noreen (née Nickelson) and Vernon McDormand, and renamed Frances Louise McDormand.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Louis William Tomlinson (<a href="/wiki/One_Direction" title="One Direction">One Direction</a>) was born Louis Troy Austin to Johannah (née Poulston) and Troy Austin. His parents split up when he was young and he took the surname of his stepfather, Mark Tomlinson.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Steven Van Zandt was born Steven Lento in <a href="/wiki/Winthrop,_Massachusetts" title="Winthrop, Massachusetts">Winthrop, Massachusetts</a>; his mother, Mary Lento, remarried when he was young, and Steven took the last name of his stepfather, William Van Zandt.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Nancy Davis, later Mrs. Nancy Reagan, was born Anne Frances Robbins; she was adopted by her stepfather, Dr. Loyal Davis, whose surname she took.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-8">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Joan Fontaine was born Joan de Beauvoir de Havilland, but as her elder sister <a href="/wiki/Olivia_de_Havilland" title="Olivia de Havilland">Olivia de Havilland</a> had taken the family surname (de Havilland), Joan (after essaying such unsatisfying stage names as Joan Burfield and Joan St. John), decided to use her stepfather (Frank Fontaine)'s surname, notwithstanding both sisters' mutual dislike of their mother's husband.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110924201149/http://www.biography.com/articles/Charlton-Heston-9337556">"Biography of Charlton Heston"</a>. <i>biography.com</i>. March 18, 2010. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.biography.com/articles/Charlton-Heston-9337556">the original</a> on September 24, 2011<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">December 11,</span> 2014</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=biography.com&amp;rft.atitle=Biography+of+Charlton+Heston&amp;rft.date=2010-03-18&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.biography.com%2Farticles%2FCharlton-Heston-9337556&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+stage+names" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/><br />Heston was born John Charles Carter, the son of Lilla (née Charlton; 1899–1994) and Russell Whitford Carter (1897–1966). When Heston was 10 years old, his parents divorced. Shortly thereafter, his mother married Chester Heston, whose surname John Charles adopted, taking his mother's maiden name (Charlton) later as his forename.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-10">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Madeline Kahn was born Madeline Gail Wolfson in Boston, Massachusetts, to Freda (née Goldberg) and Bernard B. Wolfson, a garment manufacturer. After her parents divorced, her mother married Hiller Kahn, who adopted Madeline and she took his surname.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Alan Thicke was born Alan Willis Jeffery in Kirkland Lake, Ontario, Canada. His stepfather was Dr. Brian Thicke, whose surname Alan legally adopted.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-12"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-12">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Born to Curtis and Angeline Hall, he adopted his father's forename to create a portmanteau professional name.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Daughter of <a href="/wiki/Huntley_Wright" title="Huntley Wright">Huntley Wright</a>, she adopted her father's forename as part of her portmanteau stage name.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-14"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-14">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dorchesterhistoricalsociety.org/blog/?p=685">Birth name per Dorchester Historical Society website</a>, dorchesterhistoricalsociety.org; accessed September 27, 2014.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.findagrave.com/memorial/1528">Profile</a>, findagrave.com; accessed September 27, 2014.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-16"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-16">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Stage name Johnny Cougar given to him by his manager in 1975; changed to John Cougar in 1979. Mellencamp has not used this name since 1982 and has not used the name John Cougar Mellencamp since 1989.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-17"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-17">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20081002041420/http://content.answers.com/main/content/wp/en/b/b8/Deed_poll_certificate_for_Elton_John.jpg">"Deed poll certificate for Elton John"</a>. Content.answers.com. Archived from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://content.answers.com/main/content/wp/en/b/b8/Deed_poll_certificate_for_Elton_John.jpg">the original</a> <span class="cs1-format">(PDF)</span> on October 2, 2008<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">July 13,</span> 2015</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Deed+poll+certificate+for+Elton+John&amp;rft.pub=Content.answers.com&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fcontent.answers.com%2Fmain%2Fcontent%2Fwp%2Fen%2Fb%2Fb8%2FDeed_poll_certificate_for_Elton_John.jpg&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+stage+names" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-18"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-18">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">While performing in <a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a>, he has used "The Rock" exclusively since 1997. In his career as a film and television actor, he has mainly been credited as either Dwayne Johnson or Dwayne "The Rock" Johnson.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-19">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Tiny Tim (né Herbert Khaury) had no official middle name, though some web sites report it to be "Butros", his father's first name, while during his televised wedding his middle name was given as "Buckingham". His headstone reads "Khaury/Herbert B/Tiny Tim/1932-1996". <cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.findagrave.com/cgi-bin/fg.cgi?page=pv&amp;GRid=1388&amp;PIpi=888486">"Tiny Tim photos at"</a>. Findagrave.com. 2004-04-21<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">2012-05-14</span></span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Tiny+Tim+photos+at&amp;rft.pub=Findagrave.com&amp;rft.date=2004-04-21&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.findagrave.com%2Fcgi-bin%2Ffg.cgi%3Fpage%3Dpv%26GRid%3D1388%26PIpi%3D888486&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+stage+names" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r886058088"/></span>
</li>
</ol></div>
